       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         Everyone expects her to be so resilient--but beneath her calm exterior seethe emotions beyond her control and understanding. Months post "Beneath the Surface", Sam finally has to face it all, and find a way to accept the way things have to be. Sam/Jack-uber shippy. Set around Christmas time. (Originally published 12/21/2014)
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         After a fairly crappy few months (years?) SG-1 gets sent to what should be a peaceful meet and greet. Naturally, things don't go exactly as planned, but an accident gives Sam and Jack a little time alone together. It turns out to be exactly what they've been needing. Episode tag (peripherally--if you look really hard) to "Desperate Measures". Angsty Christmas guttery-fluffery unabashed Shippiness.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         Decades after Voyager's return to the Alpha Quadrant, reporter/writer Jake Sisko tries to learn the truth about the ship's adventure and its key personnel.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         A/N: This came about from a discussion on the GW Family thread about the great hug Sam and Jack shared in
         <i>
          Heroes
         </i>
         . Somebody, I don't remember who, asked us to think of other times they might have shared that kind of hug. This is my response. I'm beginning to think this is the beginning of yet another series. Hmmm. As always, I save, savor, and answer all reviews left with an email and/or reply option.
        </p>
        <p>
         This was going to be a series, but seriously, I can only do so much fanfic writing while publishing and working on my doctorate, so this went by the wayside. Each story is complete in its own right.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

            <textarea cols="50" id="embed_code_362193169" rows="4">&lt;a href="https://archiveofourown.org/works/221870"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Embrace Me&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt; (12806 words) by &lt;a href="https://archiveofourown.org/users/Polrobin"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Polrobin&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Chapters: 6/6&lt;br /&gt;Fandom: &lt;a href="https://archiveofourown.org/tags/Stargate:%20SG-1"&gt;Stargate: SG-1&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Rating: General Audiences&lt;br /&gt;Warnings: No Archive Warnings Apply&lt;br /&gt;Relationships: Sam Carter/Jack O'Neill&lt;br /&gt;Characters: Jack O'Neill, Sam Carter, Janet Fraiser&lt;br /&gt;Additional Tags: Hurt, Comfort/Romance&lt;br /&gt;Summary: &lt;p&gt;A/N: This came about from a discussion on the GW Family thread about the great hug Sam and Jack shared in &lt;i&gt;Heroes&lt;/i&gt;. Somebody, I don't remember who, asked us to think of other times they might have shared that kind of hug. This is my response. I'm beginning to think this is the beginning of yet another series. Hmmm. As always, I save, savor, and answer all reviews left with an email and/or reply option.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;This was going to be a series, but seriously, I can only do so much fanfic writing while publishing and working on my doctorate, so this went by the wayside. Each story is complete in its own right.&lt;/p&gt;</textarea>
           </p>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         A/N: Once again Sally strikes again. She posted this question on the Sam/Jack Family thread (httpcolon double forwardslash forum dot gateworld dot netslashshowpost dotphp?p=10265830&amp;postcount=184172):
         <i>
          <b>
           1- would you think sam and/or jack would be more honest when very tired, or the opposite?
          </b>
         </i>
         That question sparked this.
        </p>
        <p>
         Set on a planet of my choosing. This is not a
         <i>
          Campfire
         </i>
         fic.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         A/N: Written for Ship Day, 2009. This is a standalone story that doesn't fit into any Campfires or Embrace Me stories – but I'm hoping you'll like it anyway. As always, I don't take feedback and reviews for granted; they are, in fact, the best pay any fanfic author can receive (well, short of Amanda reading this and deciding that I just
         <i>
          have
         </i>
         to work for her!).
        </p>
        <p>
         The title for this piece is in honor of the men and women who made the tremendous effort and sacrifice to put humans on the moon, forty years ago this month.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

This is a standalone story that doesn't fit into any Campfires or Embrace Me stories – but I'm hoping you'll like it anyway.        <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         Six hours into their captivity—more than twelve hours since Pike's abduction and almost twenty hours since Number One's last sleep cycle—she slid into the illusion without realising it.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         She looks at him with that complex expression that’s punctuated their relationship ever since Pete barged onto the scene.  The one that looks like a question, or a plea – the one he’s never really understood and has never dared pursue.
        </p>
       </blockquote>
